padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1211792">Atomikbomb_</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-27">09/27/24 18:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is pleasant! Definitely a citrus rind scent (I didn't know what "hesperidic" meant, and I looked that up following cell's review below mine; and YES, hesperidic indeed) as opposed to a juicy citrus feel. Zingy 100% of the way, matched with a spicy aromatic tone. <br />
<br />
I don't necessarily agree that this is 100% unisex (wear whatever you like, I believe in breaking rules, but I'm just describing the scent in general terms), because it has a classically masculine lack of sweetness, and there's a sort of masculine herbal vibe beneath all of the citrus. I'm extremely familiar with rosemary, having a large bush in my yard, and it isn't exactly like real rosemary (thankfully, I enjoy RM but it can easily subjucate all other smells and it's impressively strong) but it is astringent. <br />
<br />
This is decent, still smells modern, and is relatively safe/likable. It doesn't last for eons, but it's certainly not bad for a citrus-dominant fragrance.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2297415"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2297415#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279737" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/298932">cell</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-11">09/11/24 19:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Aquatic, hesperidic and salty. If you like those characteristics in a fragrance, you will definitely like this. <br />
<br />
This does not smell like anything I've encountered so far. So I don't understand the reviewers saying that this is generic. It's in the same family as other aquatic citrus freshies and may remind you of some other fragrances that share the same characteristics.<br />
<br />
For that matter, I just have to state that the saltiness here is reminiscent of Bvlgari's Aqua Pour Homme Marine.<br />
<br />
It's very curious to know that some perceive an 'egg smell' from this. Same can be said about Bvlgari Aqua Pour Homme and ADG, among others. Fortunately, I don't get that egg smell from this or any other aquatics.<br />
<br />
As with any fragrance, it may be tempting to overspray, this has a potential to be cloying and in-your-face so go easy on the trigger first.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1605092">beta-ionone</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-30">05/30/24 22:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It's your average men's freshie. Since this is an old classic, expect it to be a smidge on the mature side. But it's not animalic or dusty smelling so it's a safe blind buy and any guy can wear this and should have this in his arsenal. Since every brand has a 'blue' fragrance line, if you want something that makes people swoon or grabs attention you might wanna try a different brand. <br />
<br />
There's a note in this that a few fresh fragrances have and I think it's supposed to be an aquatic note but in high concentrations it bothers me and smells more like plastic shopping bags. I'm gonna assume it's calone? <br />
<br />
There's also so many cheap knockoffs of this so of you wanna go the low-budget route there's some Al Rehab fresh fragrances for men that smell similar. But those have even higher concentration of calone. Calone isn't necessarily bad to me, it's just in some frags it's too overwhelming.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2173070"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2173070#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2173022" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; One must appreciate this though as I believe simplicity is a good thing, I get original Acqua di Gio vibes, the difference being that this has a bigger focus on citrus notes. If you don't like lemon 🍋 do not buy this! But if you dig uncomplicated, classical manly colognes definitely do. Performance is acceptable and projection is too, specially out in the summer suns where it belongs.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2173022"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2173022#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2172625" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1761519">ZeaMoore4</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-30">05/30/24 12:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When it's summer and you're going out to do something that takes no more than 2-3 hours. This is a perfect dumb grab. Hard not to like, inoffensive, not clawing, projects fine for the 2-3 hours and it doesn't care if you're working out, lying down, or anything in between. You won't impress a lot of people with your complex fragrance. But people Will think you smell fantastic.<br />
<br />
This is a Real "Eau De Toilette". People who don't know/understand fragrance will complain about longevity. But this lasts exactly as long as it should. Eau de Toilette is an old way of saying "of water/of the water" and is ment to quickly freshen you up for a short amount of time. If you need a fragrance to last 8+ hours, a fresh summer edt will be unlikely to get anywhere close to that. 4 hours would be impressive for a fresh summer edt.  <br />
<br />
Score: 8.5/10<br />
As safe as blind buys get., as long as you like the notes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2172625"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2172625#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2171266" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; One of my favorite freshies. The opening is intense and vibrant, but the dry down is where it shines and why it still sells well to this day.<br />
<br />
I love the peppery, grapefruit musk dry down. It's a manly freshie so if that's not your thing, you might want to consider the feminine powdery, iris-dominant fragrances and steer clear of this one.<br />
<br />
This will always be in my arsenal. <br />
<br />
8.5 out of 10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2081944"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2081944#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2081394" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2081394" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheDarkAura"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036306"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2036306.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheDarkAura" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2081394ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2081394" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.85); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2036306">TheDarkAura</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-03">03/03/24 20:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It has a strong, perfumy odor -- the kind that you can practically taste that makes fragrances sickening.  It sometimes smells okay to me when I can catch the citrus, but usually it feels like an alcohol blast.  I've owned it for over 8 years, and each wear I've ended up wanting to wash it off.  As fate would have it, scents that I don't like often last forever.  This one sticks to me and doesn't wash off easily. It lasts forever and projects, so if you like the scent it's a win for you.<br />
 I might pull it up to "ok" if I change my mind, but I doubt this will ever go in the like+ for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2081394"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2081394#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2076341" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Without care, sense or dedication: something after another and nothing more...</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2039480"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2039480#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2030190" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I could see myself going to the beach with this on and just smelling absolutely radical. The citrus note is for sure the thing that makes this good, but as it dries down the blending with the woody note is fantastic. As being a EDT, this doesn't have much performance but for the few 4-6 hours I get off this fragrance it just smells fabulous. If you're in to layering, this is also really good because the strong citrus note and the woody note. I've layered it with some winter fragrances and despite the difference from the notes. The woody note really comes out and helps any other fragrance. If you want a fragrance that is just a basic and you could use everyday and get a few compliments here and there, get this and you won't be disappointed.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1957207">Hugh-Jass123</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-04">01/04/24 20:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dolce and Gabbana light Blue.<br />
<br />
I got this gifted to me back when the Eau Intense wasn’t available where I lived and I wanted to try this fragrance so badly. This fragrance has a very pleasant hard to dislike smell. Mostly lemons and citruses that are perfect for a summer day. Plus the bottle is so nice. The problem I have with this fragrance is its performance. It’s so sad that I only get 3 hours of use with this fragrance because I wanted to love it. But now I can’t wear it often like how it’s supposed to be used (as an everyday scent) it projects well but it’s over so quickly. It is good for personal encounters and dinners nothing more and disappears quickly, so if you're expecting an everyday scent I’m sorry but it just doesn’t work and is just good for a summer night out. If you want the everyday fragrance you were hoping to get, purchase the Eau Intense it has almost the same smell but lasts 4 hours more and projects better.<br />
<br />
Smell: (7.5/10)<br />
Projection: (7/10) for how long it lasts<br />
Longevity: (3/10)<br />
Overall: (6/10) 😢</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="2020682"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=2020682#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2014141" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; For summer I've been mainly wearing Acqua Di Gio, so this is where I'm coming from. <br />

The opening notes are heavy citrus and musk. The citrus is not overwhelming and artificial. It's soft and refreshing. However, the citrus dies pretty fast. The citrus gives it freshness, but the musk gives it funk, which fans of fecal/floral scents will enjoy.<br />
<br />
Based on the pyramid, no wonder the citrus was so heavy (grapefruit, bergamot, mandarin).  I didn't get any juniper off the top.<br />
<br />
1 Hour Later - The citrus is gone completely.  I'm getting some spices and maybe a tiny bit of green, but it's hard for me to smell anything other than musk<br />
<br />
From the pyramid, pepper absolutely make sense.  Perhaps the greenness I got is the rosemary or juniper, maybe it was the oakmoss.  In any event it was slight.  Personally I don't get any woodiness (Brazilian Rosewood) nor do I get incense, but frankly how could anything shine through the musk<br />
<br />
Overall - I don't like the fecal/floral genre.  Light Blue's opening is so citrusy it makes me want to stick around, but all that's waiting for me is the indefatigable funk of musk.  I do like the flanker Italian Zest, which I have reviewed separately<br />
<br />
***Scents, like tastes, are subjective. Wear what you like***</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1971909"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1971909#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1968786" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1619170">YourFragranceFriend</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-14">10/14/23 14:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>We're trying to find a new signature scent for my husband after he finished his bottle of Tom Ford Tobacco Vanille. We're going through a bag of men's fragrance samples I've saved for him. First up is Light Blue. He hates the sporty, blue, aquatic scent profile, so we were really just getting this out of the way. He said it's gross and chemically. <br />
<br />
Personally, I don't like this scent either. I find it way too punchy. I love all these notes separately; together, they are overpowering and offputting. I find the bright citrus, herbs, spices, and aromatics are all fighting for my attention without melding. There's a smooth musky and woody base that doesn't serve to bring together the punchy notes into something cohesive. It's almost so removed from the rest of the scent that it's a little nauseating. If someone were sitting next to me wearing this scent, I'd probably move away.<br />
<br />
The women's version of this fragrance succeeds in making a cohesive scent that blends bright, tart notes with a creamy base.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1951932"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1951932#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1950872" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Not complex, not even especially "fresh" to me, but certainly inoffensive and easy enough to reach for. (By the way, when I first tried this, the big ozone note reminded me of a very similar ozone element in Frederic Malle Vetiver Extraordinaire!) In any event, I prefer the original Light Blue, despite it being marketed to women.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1888052"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1888052#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1881016" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1853147" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Sniffitout"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1737579"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1737579.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Sniffitout" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Acqua-di-Gio-Profumo-29727.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.29727.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Acqua di Giò Profumo"title="Acqua di Giò Profumo"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1853147ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1853147" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1737579">Sniffitout</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-06-10">06/10/23 02:15</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The original light blue pour homme is one of the best designer aquatics on the market that I think is overshadowed by the hype of the eau intense flanker.<br />
<br />
Scent:<br />
It has an addicting fresh, salty-aquatic, juicy citrus, and airy musk smell. Fortunately, it doesn't have the wet dog type of smell that eau intense does. The original smells nothing but pleasant.<br />
<br />
Performance:<br />
It pops off my skin pretty well for the first few hours, but dries to a skin scent after 4-5 hours or so. On clothes, I can smell it past the 8 hour mark. Spray a few more sprays of this than you typically would and it'll last through a good chunk of the day.<br />
<br />
Cost:<br />
Being $30-$40 on Amazon or about 50 cents per milliliter, this is an absolute steal. The quality far outweighs the cost. I have no idea how people currently have the price rated as "ok" on Fragrantica instead of as a "great value".<br />
<br />
Comparison to eau intense:<br />
Eau intense performs better than the original, but the wet dog or dirty fish tank smell of eau intense makes it a no-go for me. Since the original lasts long enough in most situations, I'd rather compromise on performance to get its superior scent profile.<br />
<br />
Overall Ranking (using my own weighted ranking):<br />
-Scent: 46/50<br />
-Quality of blend: 12/15<br />
-Versatility: 7/10 (due to it being more fitting for warm weather)<br />
-Timelessness: 4/5<br />
-Performance (longevity, projection, sillage): 10/18<br />
-Value: 2/2<br />
<br />
Total Score: 81/100 or 8.1/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1853147"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1853147#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1845489" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Perfect Opening for most people to like. Citruses and fresh/airy. Best opening I smelled after Acqua Di Gio which opens with citruses too.<br />
There is a slight flowery/woody dry down which seems to be from Juniper/Rosemary/Rosewood combination as seen in notes. That makes this perfume much different than opening. It starts young but inclines towards bit oldish.<br />
Seems to be less projecting after 1/2 hour. I found it weak, pretty obvious, citrus/fresh scents usually are not as loud as opening.<br />
This review is based on Complete dry down on strip.<br />
On skin it gave much lesser performance but dry-down went much different than strip. Lasted only 3 hours on close to skin.<br />
<br />
P.S. It will be will be interesting to know and try some other perfume which opens exactly like this but has different dry down. I recommend all to try this just for the sake of unforgettable opening, which wiped all <br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1641148">chcatkins</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-02-03">02/03/23 16:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Yes, there is citrus in here, but this is not trying to be another citrus cologne. Unlike so many warm weather frags that make their bergamots and grapefruits and lemons the stars so that the scent is “unmistakably” fresh, Light Blue keeps them a bit tucked away with its other clean aromatics so that the black pepper can hold center stage. The incense is subtle and doesn’t add any overt smokiness, but it compliments the musk to make a very smooth, masculine base. I do wish it had a bit more of either a marine or a salty accord to make it more suitable for the deep of summer, but its restraint makes it much more useful as a signature fragrance. I am a huge fan of black pepper, and this smells fantastic on my skin. I know it’s old and basic and yadda yadda, but there’s a reason Light Blue has remained in production and this popular for so long, and there’s a reason it caught my nose so easily during my first big sampling spree. It’s versatile, it’s a people pleaser, and it deserves to be a 4+ imo.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1751076"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1751076#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1739567" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; One more thing I wanted to add, this is almost a completely different frag than the 2022 D&amp;G LB on the market rn, its deep incense, inky oakmoss, and zingy citrus with those lightly spiced woods make it almost niche-like, prolly better than some of the niche freshies I have.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1429579">JayBeez</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-30">08/30/22 17:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Found this at a great price at Sam's Club and thought I'd give it a whirl, figuring I'd return it if I didn't like it. On initial spray, it's quite similar to Light Blue for women. My first wear was a conservative 3 spray application (Adam's apple, wrists). I called it "Gone in 60 seconds" and almost took it back. I do have other weakies in my collection (I'm looking at you Fleurs de Citronnier) so opted to heavy up on the application. Turns out that's the ticket on this one. Still smells similar to LB for women at first, but after about an hour it offers up an intimate yet noticeable hint of incense and pepper that hang around for a few more hours. Been wearing it in the 90+ degree (32C) summer heat.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1634679"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1634679#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1621920" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1621920" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Freshaquatic"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1142234"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1142234.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Freshaquatic" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Louis-Vuitton/Afternoon-Swim-53947.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.53947.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Afternoon Swim "title="Afternoon Swim "></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1621920ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1621920" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1142234">Freshaquatic</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-11">08/11/22 22:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Got this as a 21st birthday gift back in 2007 and it was one of my first ever fragrances.<br />
<br />
Longevity was good enough to still be smelled over a sweaty post-nightclub tee shirt, and the dry down was more... earthy than it is now.   <br />
<br />
Seeking to revisit the old days I purchased a newer bottle in about 2018.  While most of what I remember about the  scent is still there, the soul is missing from it, the "extra" thing that elevates it from a generic citrus to an actual fragrance worthy of its popularity.  In this case, a bit of richness, fullness, and more complexity in the dry-down.<br />
<br />
Trying to work out what may be missing, and using the notes on this page I settled on Oakmoss (which I guessed was probably heavily reduced or removed due to ever-increasing IFRA restrictions over the years), and decanted some of the new juice (measured out by weight).  Estimating/guessing the original concentration, I added some oakmoss absolute at approximately 2007 IFRA-acceptable levels.  And just like that, BOOM, the magic is back!  <br />
<br />
If you have digital scales, and access to oakmoss absolute I encourage you to try it!  It doesn't completely change the scent, but gives it more body and soul, and because oakmoss is long-lasting, it dries down a bit different and lasts longer.  Sure, this is probably not the only change made to the formula over the years, but I rediscovered some of the magic I used to love in this scent which was a big part of a very exciting time in my life.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1227733">Ambroxer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-10">08/10/22 10:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I’ve had a sample of Light Blue laying around for awhile but never had any particular interest. It seemed so overshadowed by its more contemporary flankers, I just didn’t see the point. The idea struck me though, that maybe these originals that began long running lines are worth a look. So I dug that sample out. <br />
<br />
I’m glad I did because I find myself liking it more than I thought I would. I get a splash of tart citrus over more aromatic notes. An inviting musk rounds out the package and adds a touch of sensuality to the base. The overall effect provides a refreshing detour from these hottest days of August. I was also surprised at how familiar Light Blue smells without having consciously smelled it before. While longevity and projection are nothing to write home about, it’s easy to see the appeal of the fragrance and why a new version is introduced annually. <br />
<br />
This original is more straightforward than some of the flankers currently receiving hype. But hey, can’t go wrong with citrus and aromatics on a hot day. Light Blue may not be as sexy as what it’s advertising conveys anymore, but it sure delivers that laid back, beach front mood.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1620852"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1620852#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1619536" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1484136">SpiceyChicken</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-06-24">06/24/22 20:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>At first I was regretting not picking up the more talked about and suggested Eau Intense for the longest time, yes that one does naturally have better longevity. However where this one finds its purpose is during extreme high heat, peak of summer situations when you know you'll be in a sweat soon after going outside or doing activity.<br />
<br />
Starts off super clean and bright, very soapy, a bit peppery, and then the citruses comes out more when the heat gets on your skin and you sweat. You're left with soft woods and a mild musk by the tail end of it when it starts to fade. Nothing sweet about this one whatsoever(which is good).<br />
<br />
This is extremely safe, and by no means a big headturner but delicate and pretty scents like this still should be appreciated. All that being said.. don't overpay retail price for this, this one seems readily available on discounters.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1590926"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1590926#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1586398" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Its very synthetic and generic smelling. If I didn't know this was D&amp;G, i'd think it was made by a $20 department store generic knock off brand. <br />
<br />
Maybe the excessive amount of cheap and perfumed households products we have nowadays (candles, plug-ins, scented cleaners, lotions, hand soaps, etc.) have really destroyed our perception of smell and understanding of perfumery. <br />
<br />
I think Light Blue would be a decent outdoor summertime, hot weather, at the beach type perfume..but it smells too strongly similar to bathroom cleaner, and the strength of association of the memory is too much to ignore. It's bit too sharp and citrusy, and quite unpleasant in the first hour. The scent only lasted 3-4 hours on my skin, with minimal sillage after the first hour.<br />
<br />
D&amp;G Light Blue Intense is worlds better than this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1586398"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1586398#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1582943" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
I like the initial opening. The blend of citrus and whatever was in there is light and fresh without being overly lemony, orange, or obvious but shortly upon my skin, a more alcohol scent came about and the opening I liked more or less vanished. The dry down left a somewhat fresh scent but after a few hours it was gone. Feel I might like a more luxury version of this fragrance that captures the initial opening all the way through with more projection and longevity, and just more volume on the overall character. I'm curious about the other versions, but not so much I would consider blind buying them. Don't find it very masculine, more unisex. A straight face because even at it's price point a more longevity would be nice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1556175"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1556175#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1551791" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This smells more like a cologne, while VPH to me just smells like cleanliness personified. Recommend.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1519816"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1519816#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1516432" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1242784">cedrat</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-03-04">03/04/22 09:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a beautiful fragrance. It's a much more pleasant (albeit expensive) alternative to its cousin Nautica Voyage, which was launched around the same time. That one is a chemically-smelling mess, whereas this one comes off more natural.<br />
<br />
When I spray this on, I get no Juniper and the faintest whiff of rosemary and rosewood, but an overall citrus zing with a mild sharpness from the incense. The combination is hypnotic at first. The entire ensemble is mild, never getting overwhelming, screechy, or loud. My mind raced back to the 90s and aughts, and this scent is very much of its time, and an excellent example of it, along with a couple others such as RL Polo Sport and Chanel Allure Homme Sport.<br />
<br />
This will work very well in many scenarios, including casual gatherings, office wear, and the gym also. Very high on the versatility scale and overall inoffensive, beautiful frag.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1516432"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1516432#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1506777" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
The original Light Blue pour Homme smells more sophisticated by comparison. It is not as long-lasting or potent, but it is just better than the intense.<br />
<br />
That said, my overall impression is simply 'it's ok.' I'm very unlikely going to grab a full bottle of it since I'm never a fan of oceanic fragrances to begin with. But if you are a fan of marine fragrances, this and Bvlgari Aqva are both good choices. (I like Bvlgari better though.)<br />
<br />
What bothers me is the fact that the sea notes are not in the pyramid. I hate it when companies don't declare the important notes in full. It's a rather dishonest act if you ask me.<br />
<br />
If you like oceanic combined with citrus fragrances, this is a safe blind buy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1503606"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1503606#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1497084" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; So it's a bit more sensual, with the rosewood, musk, and oakmoss, than a pure citrus fragrance. For me it lasts longer than most citrus freshies and has stronger sillage. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1445956" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Brothowalee"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1413308"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Brothowalee" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1445956ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1445956" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1413308">Brothowalee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-11-14">11/14/21 18:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Does everyone ever experience testing a perfume in the store, and immediately felt love-struck?<br />
<br />
I did with this. <br />
<br />
Fragrance preference is a very delicate, personal, and extremely subjective matter. <br />
For me personally, before i encounter a light blue, my taste and knowledge of fragrance is somehow very very limited, and tend to play it safe with it. <br />
I usually choose a fresh or citrusy smell, and steer away from woody-spicy-leathery aroma. <br />
<br />
But after i took a sniff of light blue, i felt a complex sensation. It started with citrusy aroma, but with a hint of other ingredients. The combo somehow create an amazing sensation for me, not an ordinary citrus, this is a bit complex... bit intimidating at first, because i don't get used to this aroma. <br />
<br />
As i let the smell lingers on my skin, the citrus dominant top notes gradually blends with a more woody (or musky?) scent, creating a combination of powdery smell that... I don't know how to describe it... It just felt right. <br />
For me, it felt cozy, laidback vibes, fresh, warm, and a sense of refine/sophistication. The feelings grew on me the longer i smell it. <br />
<br />
At the end, the bottom notes was dominated by incense and musk, with a residue of powdery citrus. The only thing that kind of let me down was the projection was not really long. 3 to 4 hours top, and the smell really fades away with bare minimum hint of scent left. <br />
I imagine the smell could lean towards unisex, with perhaps a very limited numbers of female that would be attracted with the aroma characteristics.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1047408">fromthebayandaroundtheway</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2021-08-19">08/19/21 03:49</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Light Blue has a great opening. A cloud of: grapefruit, bergamot and mandarin orange flow out of the sprayer and quickly nestle into layer of pepper and rosewood. The effect of these notes interacting acts like a smooth cotton or fresh linen. The musk finally shows up in the faintest of ways, with a slight touch of musk and oakmoss. The effect is different, unique and certainly piques a curiosity, however the scent fades out and settles quickly into a skin scent, which is typical of most of these light, citrus summer scents. This composition is fantastic, but sadly, just very weak.<br />
Light Blue is a very relaxing scent and fits perfectly in the spring/summer rotation. This fragrance requires heavy sprays and does great for an event that occurs on a late afternoon on a spring or summer day. With Light Blue think; clean and relaxed with down time and terrace drinks on the agenda.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1394950"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1394950#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1394890" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="strike-title"><span>Most Popular Positive Reviews</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent588079" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc588079" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Vierhuizen"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/40648"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.40648.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Vierhuizen" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma588079ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd588079" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/40648">Vierhuizen</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-04-21">04/21/15 20:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dolce &amp; Gabanna Light Blue<br />
<br />
Many reviewers here say it's nothing special, I believe they are simply wording things wrong. Instead of being nothing special, I would say it's nothing particularly "new".<br />
<br />
The cologne realm is full of fresh/woodsy scents. We will both assume since you are on this website, you are aware of this fact.<br />
So what separates Light Blue from the Acqua Di Gios, Chanels, Calvin Kleins, Ralph Laurens, and others?<br />
<br />
My answer? Not much, not much at all. Is this a bad thing? That's completely up to your interpretation. When I smell Light Blue I smell fresh, light woods, paired with a little less citrus notes, and a hint of refreshing floral notes. <br />
<br />
I get anywhere between 4-6 hours out of this cologne, along with moderate silage. Above all else, I feel clean, crisp, and confident- on top of that, I garner compliments damn near every time I wear it!<br />
<br />
Groundbreaking? No. Something special? For you, maybe. For others, maybe not. <br />
<br />
That's the best part about the fresh/citrus/woodsy segment! Almost all of them smell good, and there's plenty of variety to satisfy what you're looking for! <br />
<br />
Who knows? Maybe Light Blue will hit the spot for you!<br />
<br />
Overall rating: 7/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="588079"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=588079#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent609505" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's because they smell good, like this one.<br />
<br />
I've tried my fair share of niche, vintage etc., and while I can appreciate the "art", most of them are not well received by the people around me. <br />
<br />
One might call this "generic" in that it smells like very many other fragrances in the same genre, but that isn't necessarily a bad thing. It's a smell that people can relate to and evokes a laidback state of mind.<br />
<br />
I can't count the times I've worn a rare, highly appreciated perfume in the fragrance community (let's say Patou Pour Homme), only to hear "Jesus, man, what the hell are you wearing?" I've often found pleasure in wearing a fragrance I know most people won't be wearing, but that doesn't mean I'm doing myself any favors.<br />
<br />
I've probably been somewhat of a perfume snob for a few years, but that hasn't been working out too well for my wallet or senses.<br />
<br />
In conclusion (and back to Light Blue), longevity and sillage are excellent, it smells great and chicks love it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="609505"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=609505#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent806903" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;     <div class="strike-title"><span>Most Popular Negative Reviews</span></div>
    <div class="grid-x grid-padding-x grid-margin-y" style="position: relative; padding: 0 0.25rem 0 0.25rem;">
                            <div id="parent574446" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc574446" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jerry Can"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/785126"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.785126.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jerry Can" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma574446ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd574446" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/785126">Jerry Can</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2015-03-06">03/06/15 08:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is an unusual scent. I like Light Blue, but only a long LONG way into the drydown. I danced around it a while before buying; and even then, it took a few wearings before I became completely comfortable using it.<br />
<br />
Firstly, credit where credit is due: the citrus opening is very natural with the juniper making it bitter like a rare and very dry vermouth. That's the easy bit. It's what follows that is less complimentary. The musk is much too heavy and really suffocates the rosemary, oakmoss, rosewood and incense. Arguably, the musk overload kills the whole perfume. I am drawn to incense, and in Light Blue I really wouldn't know it was there. I honestly don't notice much else, just hints rather than expressions. <br />
<br />
So, the citrus almost gives way immediately to the musk - making this rather one-dimensional. Admittedly it has a uniqueness - which is some achievement in this age of mass perfumery. All the same, the appeal is understandably not universal. If I'm reminded of anything then it is like sniffing a bag of lemon sherbets or lemon-merangue pie - but with musk and a hint of rosemary.<br />
<br />
Having said all that, Light Blue gets a whole lot better on me the longer I leave it. Just a bit of an endurance getting there. Realistically Light Blue is a warm weather fragrance. Depending on your taste and expectation this could be very good (or equally not).<br />
<br />
On deeper reflection, if I wish to wear a citrus, I'm probably more drawn to Hermes' d'Orange Verte, Miller Harris' Petit Grain, or even 4711. But I stress this a personal opinion and not a criticism of Light Blue.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="574446"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=574446#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent693283" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249909">DSC9000</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-08-31">08/31/20 17:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was a blind buy on my part. My wife regularly wears Light Blue EdT as a summer fragrance and I absolutely adore it. I found Light Blue Pour Homme for a deal at a rack store and picked it up, largely based on how much I like Light Blue EdT.<br />
<br />
The blind buy didn't work in my favor. This is an insta-headache fragrance for me. I tried multiple times with the same result. I haven't nailed down which note is causing it. I can see this being an appealing fragrance for many, just not for me.<br />
<br />
It was a good deal though and not every blind buy pans out.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="1218563"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=1218563#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent470482" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc470482" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Carles"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/85209"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.85209.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Carles" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma470482ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd470482" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/85209">Carles</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-03-27">03/27/14 12:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>On me this is SO citrusy. Unfortunately, I don't get the woody, musky notes some of you are talking about. Instead the citrus notes stick on my skin until I wash it off. It smells synthetic and like cleaning products, which makes my stomach turn. The sillage and longetivity is good though. I have the after shave but it stays on me for hours.<br />
<br />
I had hoped this would smell more like the women's Light Blue and got dissapointed when it didn't. However, I luckily found Versace eau Fraiche, which also has a citrusy opening but is well balanced with ceedar and woodsy notes that instead of enhancing the citrus, lowers it a bit and makes it pleasant.<br />
<br />
I recommend you try it on you before you buy this, as it can easily be a waste of money if you experience the same thing I do when wearing this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1068"comment_id="470482"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dolce-Gabbana/Light-Blue-pour-Homme-1068.html?ccid=470482#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="1068" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
